## 💡 General Recommendations

### Priority Actions

1. **Fix Critical Issues First** - Address all 🔴 critical failures immediately
2. **Address Failed Checks** - Work through ❌ failed checks by priority
3. **Review Suggestions** - Consider implementing ℹ️ informational suggestions

### SEO Best Practices

- Ensure every page has a unique, descriptive title (30-60 characters)
- Write compelling meta descriptions (120-155 characters)
- Use a single H1 tag per page that describes the main topic
- Structure content with proper heading hierarchy (H1 → H2 → H3)
- Add descriptive alt text to all images
- Implement structured data (JSON-LD) for rich search results
- Configure Open Graph tags for social media sharing
- Maintain a sitemap.xml and robots.txt file
- Use HTTPS and ensure canonical URLs are set
